Whether it's due to the rapid expansion, inexperienced unit and district management, or trying to cut costs, this concept is being overtaken by others. Local options in particular are capturing more marketshare because their offerings are fresher, more flavorful and quite often served by friendlier staff.
Our visit was acceptable, but nothing special. The bowls we ordered were relatively bland, but quickly prepared.

Relic Vintage is quite literally the store of my dreams; I never knew something so perfect could actually exist until I walked in and saw it all for myself. I am an aspiring dental student interested in becoming a dentist. During my time shadowing Dr. Mendoza I gained insight into his practice as well as his character, and so I thought I would share my observations.

FYI* Itooth Dentistry has a separate special room for scanning teeth to make retainers (3M TruDef Digital Scanner). My fianc√© was getting her teeth scanned to make a retainer to close a gap in her front teeth.

Carine was the hygienist who listened to my dental history and asked some logical follow up questions.  She spent about 45 minutes on my appointment, counting and numbering my teeth, measuring the gaps in between my teeth and gum line, cleaning my teeth and making recommendations for keeping my teeth and gums healthy.  There was lots to talk about in my mouth, but I heard no ridicule or judgement from the hygienist or the dentist.

I was impressed with the relaxed  and professional atmosphere of the iTooth Dentistry office.  This is a very well run dental office.   I was thoroughly impressed with the entire experience.  I will return for my bi-annual visits.</Text>< username>

< Name>
Jeff Klem</Name>
<review>Consistantly very good!

So our first visit was a few months ago when we first moved to SC. We were looking for a new Thai "go-to" close by. I came really close to giving it a 4 star review as everything was good almost very good but nothing remarkable. We had the chicken pad thai. The flavors were not quite there and a little bland compared to other Thai places we have visited in other areas.

However, on our visit Saturday night, the meal was great and Flavors vibrant!

LOCATION & AMBIANCE (Rating 3.5) Tucked away in a strip mall that is not easy to find the Thai Palace is not quite a hole in the wall, but definitely not fine dining. Both times we've been there it's been moderately busy with a good take out business it seems. Most of the seating is on the side and back of the building, so we've found that the waitresses are not very responsive as there is no line of site for them to be able to do their work and keep an eye on your needs as well.

SERVICE  (Rating 3) They have always been nice, but as mentioned above, great service is practically impossible if the waitresses have no line of site with you as they have allot of counter work to do as well.

YELLOW CURRY CHICKEN (Rating 4.5)
* First Visit (Rating 3.5) We ordered the Yellow chicken curry which was good. The sauce was heavy, in a good way and flavors were good and it did come with rice.
* 10/3/2015 (Rating 4.5) The flavors were vibrant, the spices perfectly balanced as just the right amount of potatoes were added which can defeat the spices very easily.

TAM KHA SOUP w CHICKEN (Rating 4.5)
* 10/03/2015 Visit (Rating 4.5) Tonight I found the Tam KHA soup to be excellent. The balance of sweet and spicy was superb and the soup consistency was just right. The quality of some of the cabbage used was not up to par and the chicken was just a little over cooked which happens so easily, but I'd order this again in a minute. Much better tonight than the first visit.
* First Visit (Rating 3.75) We had the Tam Kar soup with chicken as well, which was also good. Not quite as sweet as some others I've had, but very good. All of the chicken in every dish was over cooked which can happen in these types of dishes very easily. I think we'll give it another shot and revisit this rating.

CHICKEN PHAD THAI (Rating 4.25) The chicken phad thai is wonderful. They use the red noodles and it's consistency and spices used are nicely done. This dish is not spicy and to be honest it needs a little more heat, so plan on adding that.<//review>< Response>

< review>
I can't speak for other rooms in this establishment but we stayed in Room 126 and were very disappointed with several issues.
I will speak to our biggest concern which was the shower.

When we turned on the spigot the pipes in the wall rattled so hard and loud it was like a locomotive coming through the wall.  Not only was it difficult to take a shower at this level of noise- right next to your ear- but the water pressure was about half of normal (LOW) and so it took longer to complete the task.
This was not only an issue for us, but I can not imagine how the room next to us would fair if someone in 126 were to take a late evening or very early morning shower.
I phoned the girl at the front desk.  She was familiar with the issue and gave me the pat response:  I am so sorry for your inconvenience.  I will have them look at it again, but it is a problem with HIGH water pressure.   And that was it.
Since this was probably a low/level/wage employee I decided to deal with it at check out.

Next morning the man at the desk asked me if we enjoyed our stay.
I replied in as polite a tone I could manage-  Do you really want to know?
He didn't say a word and kept on completing the check out.

Why ask if you all you want to hear is, yes?

After a long pause I told him Room 126 never should have been rented.
Nor was this fair to people who would stay in the next room.
His coworker's response was they put it on their list and would take care of it.
No reduction in the room charge, nor an apology.

The shower was a problem yet the way it was handled was worse.

Next visit, for $169, we will drive a few miles farther and stay at the Sofitel.< /review>

Made my way in to Willo Beauty Bar this last Sunday afternoon! Wow, what an experience!! It was my first time at this particular salon, but I've followed my stylist Morganne for the last few years and she's now currently a part of the Willo family! For starters, it's in the Loehmann's Plaza in Sacramento, where many other shops & restaurants are conveniently located right outside the salon. In my case, it provided much to do for my husband & son while I got a couple hrs of "me" time.

Anyways, back to the salon. Everyone was super friendly and helpful. The place has a very classy & relaxing vibe to it. The first thing you see when you walk in is this long bar down the middle of the salon, with mirrors and chairs lined all the way down. Not your average salon set up. But quite honestly, I really liked it!

Morganne did a spectacular job, as usual! I went in to get my ombr√© touched up. She lightened the blonde, brought it up higher, pulled out the brassiness in my hair, styled my bangs, and gave me a much needed cut. I absolutely love it! Perfect look for summer! She was super friendly the entire time, and did all that I asked for. Prices stayed true to what I was quoted from the start. Which is nice!

Overall great experience with both my stylist Morganne and the salon in general! I'll continue to go here from now on and I'd highly recommend it to anyone else :)< /Review>

Food is excellent and my fave place to order from when in Sacramento. However, the same dishes are different each time... These comments relate to orders sent through DoorDash and not placed in person.</review>
